<UserId.>111644673136196029337< /UserId.>< Review>
PetSmart is a large pet supply store with caring, knowledgeable employees. Jeremy, the assistant store manager, spent over an hour helping my wife and myself select and fit a harness, collar and leash for our dog.

‚úìCats and dogs, available for adoption, are given prominent, air-conditioned space at the front of the store. It gets hot in Encino. Small live animals and fish are available for sale.

So you adopt a companion.  One you can pick up in one hand. Really cute. After a week, your arm feels two inches longer and the tug boat you've adopted is trying to eat the couch. You need help my friend, you and your companion need a trainer. So, you ask a few friends and get recommends for a trainer who cost about as much as your mortgage.  Obviously, you and your buddy need group therapy.

‚úìThat's what PetSmart offers at a reasonable price.  Five Lessons currently cost a litte over one hundred dollars (us). Cookie, our dog friend, loves her trainer, Jasmin. She is kind, and caring. After five classes, she has learned to sit, lay down, come when called, and to walk without pulling. My arm has return to normal.

‚úìPetSart also offers pet grooming at reasonable prices.

‚úìNew owners of adopted pets are presented a coupon booklet offering significant discounts. Proof of adoption is required.  Free parking. Everything is wheelchair accessible.

Several restaurants in the shopping complex offer outdoor seating so you and your companion can enjoy some time together.</Review>

<Text>This is a first Authentic Italian Restaurant that I have been to since being in Italy. The environment is very nice and quiet. They have a small section for larger group/table and the main dining area. Another intriguing point is the wine cellar dining experience, this should be fun. The "Authentic Italian Cuisine" means that the dishes have NOT been Americanized. They are produced from original Italian recipes, no short cuts allowed. Delicious!!!

Our meal was exquisite. My ribeye was grilled to perfection, the sole was light and flakey. and the pork loin was so tender you could cut it with a fork.

The wine selection is top notch and we were told that the collection will be thorough, extensive and most remarkable, "every wine is by the glass"! This means I could have a '98 Borolo and not have to fork over for an entire bottle.

The restaurant's staff is thorough and an absolute delight. Everyone that interacted with us were from Italy, so this gave even more authenticity. The desserts were not all standard fare. I had my first "Grandmother's cake" and a Chocolate wonder (Lava Cake). I was told that normally it would have chili peppers incorporated, but the worry was it was too soon for people to appreciate it. However, I appreciated it very much, with our without the chilis.

And of course, I finished my meal with a double espresso that had a wonderfully smooth taste and presented with a beautiful cr√®me.

All in all, a great dinner, great space, great people and I look forward to making the trip from the Bay Area at least once per month if not more. I am looking forward to seeing the restaurant evolve and it has just opened and the menu and wines are sure to mature and change.

<user_id>102460323036340728985</user_id>< Text>
If it is not the only poke place in college area(and in the whole east county), I would advise any poke lover against this place. The food was alright, the freshness and taste were both okay, but compared to all the other poke spots I have been to all over California, they have a rather small selection of ingredients, there were only three options for proteins, salmon, tuna and tofu, and if you want to add a small scoop of spicy tuna, that's an extra two dollars. Unlike most poke place that offer unlimited topping, they charge extra even for a lot of regular items like seaweed or fried onion. Given these facts, their price is also a little too high, 11 dollars for a small bowl, and that's without any add-on. If you want to have as many proteins and topping you usually get from other poke place, you could easily end up with over 15 dollars for a bowl, and that is crazy for poke.<//Text>
